###Life cycle, Automation, Tabs. What we want to do ####At the end of the course: - Add action to borrow a book - Add a new tab to see only the borrowed books of a BookLibrary ![Tabs bring back](img/tabs-bring-back.png) - Add a new tab for Book document with - the list of books or the same author - the actions borrow or bringback - the state of the document - a toggleable layout to view and edit the book metadatas - the default edit and summary tab would be disabled
Nuxeo Training - Life cycle =============== ######S.TAN - A.KERVERN
###Life cycle - Builtin core feature
All document in Nuxeo has a lifecycle and a state
- State of a document - Allowed transitions from a state to another - Initial state - A life cycle policy for each doc type

###Life cycle (w/o studio) Core API 2 core actions available
From Nuxeo Core about life cycle. We'll see later how we can call them
- Follow a transition: CoreSession#followTransition(DocumentRef docRef, String transition) - Get the current life cycle state: CoreSession#getCurrentLifeCycleState(DocumentRef docRef) returns String
### Note: The trash folder The deleted state and the delete transition are used to have the trash feature on the document whatever the lifecycle is. If you want to activate the trash feature on a document type that uses a custom lifecycle, you must add those state and transition in the custom lifecycle

Nuxeo Training - User actions and automation chains ======================== ######S.TAN - A.KERVERN
Automation chains and operations --------------------------
###Operations
Unitary and reusable operators that implement a particular documentary function, such as "move a document", "update a property", "change the lifecycle state", "transform to PDF", "send as email"...
####An operation is defined by - A unique name - Input contents - Ouput contents - Process (can contain parameters) #### Accepted input and output - Document - List of Document - Blob - List of Blob - void
### Example: Follow transition ####For instance, the "Follow Life Cycle transition" - Name: Document.SetLifeCycle - Input: Documents,Document - Output: Documents,Document - Parameter: Transition the name of the transition to follow - Process: - follow the transition in parameter to the input document - returns the modified document
###Automation chains Chains operations - Build business logic by chaining - Output should fit the next operation input - Studio checks operation inputs and outputs - launched from user actions, events or REST
###Automation Chain
###A Chain in Studio - Ordered set of operations - Respecting input and output of operations - Sharing a context in the whole chain, with variables - Some chains are aware of the UI context, some are not. - The chain takes as input the UI Current Document or the document bound to the Event Handler (see after)
###A chain in Studio ![Studio automation UI](img/automation-studio.png)
###Available operations - Categories - Documents - Execution flow - Fetch - Services - etc ...
##Using automation for creating, updating and moving data
### Fetching Documents ####Initialize the input of your chain - by Id or Path - Fetch > Document operation - Id: aced8d8f-4780-45e0-9605-b0d96119bb89 - Path: /default-domain/workspaces/ta-slides-and-docs - by a NXQL query - Fetch > Query operation - by the contextual document (default fetch)
which is either the current document in the UI or the document bound to the event, depending on the context of execution of the chain
- Some specific UI contextual document - Fetch > UI CurrentWorkspace, - Fetch > UI Current Domain, - ...
###XPath: handle metadata values - xpath to identify metadata property - in operation parameters Document > Update Property - ex: dc:title (dublincore title), dc:subjects, uid:uid - schema_prefix:property - Get properties from Mvel Document object Document['dc:title']
Can be used with Document object in scripted expressions of operation parameters: Document[dc:title] will return the title of the document that was in input of the operation (dc is the prefix of the Dublincore schema)
###Useful operation - Document > Create: create a document right below the input one - Document > Update Property, Document Update Properties - Document > Move - Document > Copy, Document > Publish Document - Document > Delete
###Inject dynamic values with MVEL - In operation parameters: @{mvel script evaluated} - Objects browser in Studio, from each operation parameters
will help you use the good syntax
- Object Fn, the Document Wrapper, the Date Wrapper. - MVEL http://mvel.codehaus.org/Getting+Started+for+2.0
###Fn Object Collection of useful helpers
available in automation parameters when using the script ( @{ script_expression})
- getNextId(string)
returns the next sequence item for the given string (enables to maintain in parallel multiple sequences)
- getDate()
return a Date object from a date property
- getVocabularyLabel(VocabularyName, KeyName)
returns the label for a vocabulary entry. (ex: useful when automatically updating some fields)
- getEmailsFromGroup(String groupName), getEmails, ...
useful helpers for resolving users, emails, etc, ...

Exercise - User actions and automation chains

Sun Seng David TAN
###Exercise User actions and automation Add a button to change the lifecycle state to "borrowed" and update a new field "Borrowed by" with the name of the current user - Add a new metadata to your book named borrowedBy only visible (can't modify) - Update your schema - Update your layout - Create a new automation chain that - Fetch the current document - Follow the lifecycle transition borrow - automatically fill the new field borrowedBy with the current user name - Create an action linked to the chain that is visible for Book document with a InLibrary state
###Exercise: Something more difficult? (optional) - Add a new field to your book named borrowedAt (Date), you need to filled it during the previous operation and must appear to be in read only and not visible when creating a Book. - Add a new state named revived on our life cycle - Create a new operation chain that: - Fetch documents that have been borrowed 3 months ago (30 sec in our case ) - Set books state as revived. - Send an email to all borrowers to get back the book
Tab Designer ----------------- ###### S.TAN
###Tabs in Nuxeo - Tabs in the document type definition - define tabs with content views - Tabs designer - define tabs with the designer
###Tabs for just content views ![Tabs of content views](img/tabs-doctype.png)
###Tab designer - Section Listings & Views > Tabs in Studio ![tabs-tabdesigner-section](img/tabs-tabdesigner-section.png) - Can insert widgets such as: - Content views - Toggleble layouts - actions from a category - metadata fields - More customizable rows - Enablement tab - By default, always display - Can filter by doc types, lifecycle state, etc ...
